Team Collaboration Features\n\nFORGE supports multi-user collaboration through server mode, allowing multiple users to observe and interact with the same FORGE instance.\n\n## Overview\n\nTeam collaboration features enable:\n- Multiple users can observe the same FORGE instance\n- Role-based access (viewer vs operator vs admin)\n- Named user sessions with attribution on actions\n- Shared bead queue with assignment\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Server Mode\n\nWhen FORGE runs in server mode, it hosts a WebSocket server that clients can connect to for real-time state synchronization.\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  FORGE Server (Host)                                     │\n│  - WebSocket server (ws://host:8080/ws)                 │\n│  - Session management                                   │\n│  - Bead assignment tracking                            │\n│  - State broadcast to all clients                      │\n└──────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┘\n               │\n               ↓ WebSocket\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  Clients (Multiple)                                      │\n│  - Viewer: Read-only observation                        │\n│  - Operator: Can spawn/kill workers, assign tasks       │\n│  - Admin: Full access including config changes          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n### Starting the Server\n\nStart FORGE in server mode:\n\n```bash\nforge --server\n```\n\nThe server will start on `127.0.0.1:8080` by default. You can configure the bind address and port in `~/.forge/config.yaml`:\n\n```yaml\nserver:\n  enabled: true\n  bind_address: \"0.0.0.0\"\n  port: 8080\n```\n\n### Connecting as a Client\n\nConnect to a running FORGE server:\n\n```bash\nforge --connect ws://server-host:8080/ws\n```\n\nYou can also configure connection settings in `~/.forge/config.yaml`:\n\n```yaml\nserver:\n  mode: \"client\"\n  remote_url: \"ws://server-host:8080/ws\"\n  auth_user: \"username\"\n  auth_password: \"password\"\n```\n\n## Default Users\n\nThe server comes with three default users for development:\n\n| Username | Password | Role    | Permissions                         |\n|----------|----------|---------|-------------------------------------|\n| admin    | admin123 | Admin   | Full access including user management |\n| operator | operator123 | Operator | Spawn/kill workers, assign tasks  |\n| viewer   | viewer123 | Viewer  | Read-only observation               |\n\n## Roles and Permissions\n\n### Viewer\n- View all workers, tasks, and metrics\n- No ability to modify state\n- Ideal for observation-only access\n\n### Operator\n- All Viewer permissions\n- Spawn and kill workers\n- Assign and unassign tasks\n- Modify task status\n- Cannot modify configuration or manage users\n\n### Admin\n- All Operator permissions\n- Modify configuration\n- Manage users\n- Full system access\n\n## Features\n\n### Sessions View\n\nPress `s` to view the Sessions panel, which shows:\n- Connected users\n- User roles (color-coded)\n- Current view being observed by each user\n- Connection status\n\n### Bead Assignment\n\nOperators and Admins can assign beads to specific users:\n- Assign bead from Tasks view\n- Attribution tracked (who assigned to whom)\n- Unassign beads to return to pool\n\n### Real-time Updates\n\nAll clients receive real-time updates for:\n- Worker status changes\n- Bead status changes\n- Bead assignments\n- User join/leave events\n- Cost updates\n\n### Action Attribution\n\nActions performed by users are attributed in:\n- Audit logs (who did what when)\n- Bead assignments (assigned by/to tracking)\n- Worker spawn/kill operations\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Server Configuration\n\n```yaml\nserver:\n  # Enable server mode\n  enabled: true\n\n  # Bind address (0.0.0.0 for all interfaces)\n  bind_address: \"127.0.0.1\"\n\n  # Port for WebSocket server\n  port: 8080\n```\n\n### Client Configuration\n\n```yaml\nserver:\n  # Client mode settings\n  mode: \"client\"\n  remote_url: \"ws://server-host:8080/ws\"\n\n  # Authentication credentials\n  auth_user: \"username\"\n  auth_password: \"password\"\n```\n\n## Security Considerations\n\n### Production Deployment\n\nFor production use:\n1. **Replace SimpleAuth**: The default auth provider uses hardcoded passwords. Integrate with your existing auth system (OAuth, LDAP, etc.)\n2. **Use TLS/WSS**: Encrypt WebSocket connections in production\n3. **Network Security**: Use firewall rules to restrict access\n4. **Audit Logging**: Ensure audit logs are enabled for compliance\n\n### Authentication Provider\n\nThe `SimpleAuth` provider is for development only. Implement the `AuthProvider` trait for production:\n\n```rust\n#[async_trait]\npub trait AuthProvider: Send + Sync {\n    async fn authenticate(&self, user_id: &str, credentials: &str)\n        -> Result<AuthResult, ServerError>;\n}\n```\n\n## API Reference\n\n### Server Messages\n\nMessages sent from server to clients:\n\n- `Welcome`: Session info and server state\n- `StateUpdate`: Full state snapshot\n- `UserJoined`: New user connected\n- `UserLeft`: User disconnected\n- `BeadAssigned`: Bead assigned to user\n- `WorkerChanged`: Worker status changed\n- `BeadChanged`: Bead status changed\n- `ChatMessage`: Chat message from another user\n- `Error`: Error occurred\n- `Ping`: Keep-alive ping\n\n### Client Messages\n\nMessages sent from client to server:\n\n- `Authenticate`: Authentication credentials\n- `SyncState`: Request full state sync\n- `AssignBead`: Assign bead to user\n- `UnassignBead`: Unassign bead\n- `SpawnWorker`: Spawn new worker\n- `KillWorker`: Kill a worker\n- `ChangeBeadStatus`: Modify bead status\n- `ChatMessage`: Send chat message\n- `UpdateView`: Update current view\n- `Pong`: Ping response\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Refused\n- Verify server is running: `forge --server`\n- Check firewall rules\n- Verify correct host/port\n\n### Authentication Failed\n- Verify username/password\n- Check user role permissions\n- Ensure user exists in auth provider\n\n### State Not Syncing\n- Check WebSocket connection is active\n- Verify client is subscribed to state updates\n- Check server logs for errors\n\n## Development\n\n### Running Tests\n\n```bash\ncargo test --package forge-server --test team_collaboration_test\n```\n\n### Code Organization\n\n- `crates/forge-server/src/lib.rs` - Main server exports\n- `crates/forge-server/src/auth.rs` - Authentication and authorization\n- `crates/forge-server/src/session.rs` - Session management\n- `crates/forge-server/src/assignment.rs` - Bead assignment tracking\n- `crates/forge-server/src/protocol.rs` - WebSocket protocol messages\n- `crates/forge-server/src/websocket.rs` - WebSocket server implementation\n- `crates/forge-server/src/client.rs` - WebSocket client implementation\n- `crates/forge-tui/src/sessions_panel.rs` - TUI Sessions view\n\n## Future Enhancements\n\nPotential improvements for team collaboration:\n\n1. **Persistent Auth**: Integration with OAuth, SAML, LDAP\n2. **Encrypted Connections**: TLS/WSS support\n3. **Chat System**: Built-in team chat within FORGE\n4. **Presence Indicators**: Show what each user is viewing/working on\n5. **Session Recording**: Record and replay sessions for training\n6. **Multi-Server Federation**: Connect multiple FORGE instances\n\n---\n\n**FORGE** - Federated Orchestration & Resource Generation Engine\n","numLines":270,"startLine":1,"totalLines":270}}}

Server port (default: 8080)\n64\t    #[arg(long, default_value = \"8080\")]\n65\t    server_port: u16,\n66\t\n67\t    /// Enable client mode and connect to a FORGE server\n68\t    #[arg(long,  /// Password for server authentication\n76\t    #[arg(long, value_name = \"PASSWORD\")]\n77\t    password: Option<String>,\n78\t\n79\t    /// Subcommands\n80\t    #[command(subcommand)]\n81\t    command: Option<Commands>,\n82\t}\n83\t\n84\t#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\n85\tenum Commands {\n86\t    /// Initialize FORGE configuration (first-time setup)\n87\t    Init {\n88\t        /// Run in non-interactive mode (for CI/automation)\n89\t        /// Auto-selects first available backend or uses FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND env var\n90\t        #[arg(long)]\n91\t        non_interactive: bool,\n92\t\n93\t        /// Force re-initialization even if config exists\n94\t        #[arg(long)]\n95\t        force: bool,\n96\t\n97\t        /// Re-run setup on existing config (backs up config first)\n98\t        /// Use this to change settings while preserving user data (logs, costs, status)\n99\t        #[arg(long, conflicts_with = \"force\")]\n100\t        reconfigure: bool,\n101\t\n102\t        /// Only detect available CLI tools and show results (dry run)\n103\t        /// Does not modify any files\n104\t        #[arg(long, conflicts_with_all = [\"force\", \"reconfigure\"])]\n105\t        detect_tools: bool,\n106\t    },\n107\t\n108\t    /// Update forge binary from a URL\n109\t    Update {\n110\t        /// URL to download the new binary from\n111\t        url: String,\n112\t\n113\t        /// Expected SHA256 checksum of the binary\n114\t        checksum: String,\n115\t\n116\t        /// Filename to save in staging (defaults to \"forge\")\n117\t        #[arg(short, long, default_value = \"forge\")]\n118\t        filename: String,\n119\t    },\n120\t\n121\t    /// Rollback to the previous version\n122\t    Rollback,\n123\t\n124\t    /// Clean the staging directory\n125\t    CleanStaging,\n126\t\n127\t    /// Manage workers\n128\t    Worker {\n129\t        #[command(subcommand)]\n130\t        action: WorkerAction,\n131\t    },\n132\t\n133\t    /// Validate FORGE configuration\n134\t    Validate {\n135\t        /// Show detailed validation results\n136\t        #[arg(long, short = 'v')]\n137\t        verbose: bool,\n138\t\n139\t        /// Attempt automatic fixes for issues\n140\t        #[arg(long)]\n141\t        fix: bool,\n142\t\n143\t        /// Skip chat backend connectivity test\n144\t        #[arg(long)]\n145\t        skip_backend_test: bool,\n146\t\n147\t        /// Output results as JSON\n148\t        #[arg(long)]\n149\t        json: bool,\n150\t    },\n151\t}\n152\t\n153\t#[derive(Subcommand, Debug)]\n154\tenum WorkerAction {\n155\t    /// Pause a worker (stop claiming new tasks)\n156\t    Pause {\n157\t        /// Worker ID to pause, or \"all\" to pause all workers\n158\t        id: String,\n159\t    },\n160\t\n161\t    /// Resume a paused worker\n162\t    Resume {\n163\t        /// Worker ID to resume, or \"all\" to resume all workers\n164\t        id: String,\n165\t    },\n166\t}\n167\t\n168\tfn main() -> ExitCode {\n169\t    // CRITICAL: Check for rollback BEFORE parsing CLI or initializing anything\n170\t    // This must be the first thing we do to detect crashes from previous updates\n171\t    #[cfg(feature = \"self-update\")]\n172\t    {\n173\t        use forge_core::RollbackResult;\n174\t\n175\t        match forge_core::check_and_rollback() {\n176\t            RollbackResult::RolledBack {\n177\t                failed_version,\n178\t                restored_version,\n179\t            } => {\n180\t                let restored = restored_version\n181\t                    .map(|v| format!(\"v{}\", v))\n182\t                    .unwrap_or_else(|| \"previous version\".to_string());\n183\t                eprintln!(\n184\t                    \"⚠️  Update to v{} failed on startup - rolled back to {}\",\n185\t                    failed_version, restored\n186\t                );\n187\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Update failed, rolled back to previous version\");\n188\t                eprintln!(\"Please check ~/.forge/logs/forge.log for error details\\n\");\n189\t                // Continue running with the rolled-back version\n190\t            }\n191\t            RollbackResult::Failed(err) => {\n192\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Critical: Rollback failed: {}\", err);\n193\t                eprintln!(\"You may need to manually restore from backup\\n\");\n194\t                // Continue anyway - better to try running than to abort\n195\t            }\n196\t            RollbackResult::NotNeeded => {\n197\t                // Normal startup, no crash detected\n198\t            }\n199\t        }\n200\t    }\n201\t\n202\t    // Mark that we're starting up (for crash detection on next run)\n203\t    #[cfg(feature = \"self-update\")]\n204\t    {\n205\t        if let Err(e) = forge_core::mark_startup_in_progress() {\n206\t            eprintln!(\"Warning: Failed to create startup marker: {}\", e);\n207\t            // Don't fail startup just because of this\n208\t        }\n209\t    }\n210\t\n211\t    let cli = Cli::parse();\n212\t\n213\t    // Initialize logging\n214\t    let _guard = match setup_logging(&cli) {\n215\t        Ok(guard) => guard,\n216\t        Err(e) => {\n217\t            eprintln!(\"Failed to initialize logging: {}\", e);\n218\t            return ExitCode::from(1);\n219\t        }\n220\t    };\n221\t\n222\t    // Check if this is a freshly exec'd process that needs to install itself\n223\t    #[cfg(feature = \"self-update\")]\n224\t    {\n225\t        match forge_core::check_and_perform_self_install() {\n226\t            Ok(Some(install_path)) => {\n227\t                eprintln!(\"✅ Update installed successfully to: {}\", install_path.display());\n228\t                eprintln!(\"🚀 Restarting FORGE with new version...\\n\");\n229\t                info!(\"Self-install completed to {:?}\", install_path);\n230\t                // Continue with normal startup\n231\t            }\n232\t            Ok(None) => {\n233\t                // Normal startup, not an auto-restart\n234\t            }\n235\t            Err(e) => {\n236\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Self-install failed: {}\", e);\n237\t                error!(\"Self-install error: {}\", e);\n238\t                return ExitCode::from(1);\n239\t            }\n240\t        }\n241\t    }\n242\t\n243\t    #[cfg(not(feature = \"self-update\"))]\n244\t    {\n245\t        // No self-update feature, skip installation check\n246\t    }\n247\t\n248\t    // Handle subcommands that don't require the TUI\n249\t    if let Some(command) = &cli.command {\n250\t        match command {\n251\t            Commands::Init {\n252\t                non_interactive,\n253\t                force,\n254\t                reconfigure,\n255\t                detect_tools,\n256\t            } => {\n257\t                return handle_init_command(*non_interactive, *force, *reconfigure, *detect_tools);\n258\t            }\n259\t            Commands::Worker { action } => {\n260\t                return handle_worker_action(action);\n261\t            }\n262\t            Commands::Validate {\n263\t                verbose,\n264\t                fix,\n265\t                skip_backend_test,\n266\t                json,\n267\t            } => {\n268\t                return handle_validate_command(*verbose, *fix, *skip_backend_test, *json);\n269\t            }\n270\t            _ => {\n271\t                // Other commands fall through to TUI startup\n272\t            }\n273\t        }\n274\t    }\n275\t\n276\t    // Install panic hook to ensure terminal cleanup\n277\t    install_panic_hook();\n278\t\n279\t    // Check if onboarding is needed\n280\t    if needs_onboarding() {\n281\t        eprintln!(\"🚀 Welcome to FORGE!\");\n282\t        eprintln!(\"No configuration found. Running first-time setup...\\n\");\n283\t\n284\t        if let Err(e) = run_onboarding(false, None) {\n285\t            eprintln!(\"❌ Onboarding failed: {}\", e);\n286\t            eprintln!(\"You can manually create ~/.forge/config.yaml or try again.\");\n287\t            return ExitCode::from(1);\n288\t        }\n289\t\n290\t        eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Setup complete! Starting FORGE dashboard...\\n\");\n291\t    }\n292\t\n293\t    // Validate config file if it exists\n294\t    if !needs_onboarding()\n295\t        && let Err(e) = validate_config()\n296\t    {\n297\t        eprintln!(\"\\n{}\", e);\n298\t        return ExitCode::from(1);\n299\t    }\n300\t\n301\t    // Check for required dependencies\n302\t    if !forge_core::check_dependencies() {\n303\t        // check_dependencies already prints error messages\n304\t        return ExitCode::from(1);\n305\t    }\n306\t\n307\t    info!(\"Starting FORGE dashboard\");\n308\t\n309\t    // Check if server mode is enabled\n310\t    if cli.server {\n311\t        return run_server_mode(cli.server_bind, cli.server_port);\n312\t    }\n313\t\n314\t    // Check if client mode is enabled\n315\t    if let Some(server_url) = &cli.connect {\n316\t        return run_client_mode(\n317\t            server_url.clone(),\n318\t            cli.user.unwrap_or_else(|| \"viewer\".to_string()),\n319\t            cli.password.unwrap_or_else(|| \"viewer123\".to_string()),\n320\t        );\n321\t    }\n322\t\n323\t    // Mark startup as successful (app initialized without crashing)\n324\t    #[cfg(feature = \"self-update\")]\n325\t    {\n326\t        if let Err(e) = forge_core::mark_startup_successful() {\n327\t            error!(\"Failed to mark startup as successful: {}\", e);\n328\t            // Don't fail just because of this\n329\t        }\n330\t    }\n331\t\n332\t    // Log terminal dimensions for debugging\n333\t    if let Ok((cols, rows)) = crossterm::terminal::size() {\n334\t        info!(\"Terminal size: {}x{} (columns x rows)\", cols, rows);\n335\t        eprintln!(\"Terminal size: {}x{} (columns x rows)\", cols, rows);\n336\t    } else {\n337\t        error!(\"Failed to get terminal size\");\n338\t    }\n339\t\n340\t    // Run the TUI application\n341\t    match run_app() {\n342\t        Ok(()) => {\n343\t            info!(\"FORGE dashboard exited normally\");\n344\t            ExitCode::SUCCESS\n345\t        }\n346\t        Err(e) => {\n347\t            error!(\"FORGE dashboard error: {}\", e);\n348\t            eprintln!(\"Error: {}\", e);\n349\t            ExitCode::from(1)\n350\t        }\n351\t    }\n352\t}\n353\t\n354\t/// Install a panic hook that restores the terminal before printing the panic message.\n355\t///\n356\t/// This ensures that even if the application panics while in raw mode with the\n357\t/// alternate screen enabled, the terminal will be properly restored so the user\n358\t/// can see the panic message and continue using their terminal.\n359\tfn install_panic_hook() {\n360\t    let original_hook = panic::take_hook();\n361\t\n362\t    panic::set_hook(Box::new(move |panic_info| {\n363\t        // Attempt to restore terminal state\n364\t        let _ = restore_terminal();\n365\t\n366\t        // Call the original panic hook to print the panic message\n367\t        original_hook(panic_info);\n368\t    }));\n369\t}\n370\t\n371\t/// Restore terminal to its normal state.\n372\t///\n373\t/// This function is called both on normal exit and during panic handling.\n374\tfn restore_terminal() -> std::io::Result<()> {\n375\t    let mut stdout = std::io::stdout();\n376\t\n377\t    // Disable raw mode first\n378\t    let _ = crossterm::terminal::disable_raw_mode();\n379\t\n380\t    // Leave alternate screen and disable mouse capture\n381\t    crossterm::execute!(\n382\t        stdout,\n383\t        crossterm::terminal::LeaveAlternateScreen,\n384\t        crossterm::event::DisableMouseCapture\n385\t    )?;\n386\t\n387\t    // Show cursor\n388\t    crossterm::execute!(stdout, crossterm::cursor::Show)?;\n389\t\n390\t    // Flush to ensure all escape sequences are written\n391\t    stdout.flush()?;\n392\t\n393\t    Ok(())\n394\t}\n395\t\n396\t/// Set up logging based on CLI arguments.\n397\tfn setup_logging(cli: &Cli) -> forge_core::Result<LogGuard> {\n398\t    // Initialize logging with the specified log directory\n399\t    // Either --debug or -v/--verbose enables debug logging\n400\t    let debug = cli.debug || cli.verbose > 0;\n401\t    init_logging(cli.log_dir.clone(), debug)\n402\t}\n403\t\n404\t/// Check if onboarding is needed (no config.yaml exists).\n405\tfn needs_onboarding() -> bool {\n406\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n407\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n408\t    !config_path.exists()\n409\t}\n410\t\n411\t/// Get the FORGE directory path (~/.forge).\n412\tfn get_forge_dir() -> std::path::PathBuf {\n413\t    dirs::home_dir()\n414\t        .expect(\"Could not determine home directory\")\n415\t        .join(\".forge\")\n416\t}\n417\t\n418\t/// Run the onboarding flow.\n419\t///\n420\t/// # Arguments\n421\t///\n422\t/// * `non_interactive` - If true, suppress output and auto-select backend\n423\t/// * `preferred_backend` - Optional backend to use (from FORGE_CHAT_BACKEND env var)\n424\tfn run_onboarding(\n425\t    non_interactive: bool,\n426\t    preferred_backend: Option<&str>,\n427\t) -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {\n428\t    info!(\n429\t        \"Starting onboarding flow (non_interactive={}, preferred_backend={:?})\",\n430\t        non_interactive, preferred_backend\n431\t    );\n432\t\n433\t    // Detect CLI tools with diagnostics\n434\t    if !non_interactive {\n435\t        eprintln!(\"🔍 Detecting available CLI tools...\");\n436\t    }\n437\t    let (tools, diagnostics) = detection::detect_cli_tools_with_diagnostics()?;\n438\t\n439\t    // Filter to only show tools that are ready to use\n440\t    let ready_tools: Vec<_> = tools.iter().filter(|t| t.is_ready()).collect();\n441\t\n442\t    if ready_tools.is_empty() {\n443\t        // Use the guidance module to show detailed instructions (both interactive and non-interactive)\n444\t        eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n445\t        return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n446\t    }\n447\t\n448\t    // Select the backend to use\n449\t    let selected_tool: detection::CliToolDetection = if let Some(backend) = preferred_backend {\n450\t        // Try to find the specified backend\n451\t        let normalized_backend = normalize_backend_name(backend);\n452\t        let found = tools.iter().find(|t| {\n453\t            let tool_name = normalize_backend_name(&t.name);\n454\t            tool_name == normalized_backend\n455\t        });\n456\t\n457\t        match found {\n458\t            Some(tool) => {\n459\t                if !tool.is_ready() {\n460\t                    eprintln!(\n461\t                        \"error: Backend '{}' is not ready: {}\",\n462\t                        backend,\n463\t                        tool.status_message()\n464\t                    );\n465\t                    if tool.status == detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey\n466\t                        && let Some(env_var) = &tool.api_key_env_var\n467\t                    {\n468\t                        eprintln!(\"Set the {} environment variable and try again\", env_var);\n469\t                    }\n470\t                    return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' is not ready\", backend).into());\n471\t                }\n472\t                tool.clone()\n473\t            }\n474\t            None => {\n475\t                eprintln!(\"error: Backend '{}' not found\", backend);\n476\t                eprintln!(\n477\t                    \"Available backends: {}\",\n478\t                    tools\n479\t                        .iter()\n480\t                        .map(|t| t.name.as_str())\n481\t                        .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n482\t                        .join(\", \")\n483\t                );\n484\t                return Err(format!(\"Backend '{}' not found\", backend).into());\n485\t            }\n486\t        }\n487\t    } else if non_interactive {\n488\t        // Auto-select the first ready tool in non-interactive mode\n489\t        match tools.iter().find(|t| t.is_ready()) {\n490\t            Some(tool) => tool.clone(),\n491\t            None => {\n492\t                // Tools exist but none are ready - show specific guidance\n493\t                let not_ready: Vec<_> = tools\n494\t                    .iter()\n495\t                    .filter(|t| !t.is_ready())\n496\t                    .map(|t| {\n497\t                        let (missing_api_key, incompatible_version, missing_feature) = match t.status {\n498\t                            detection::ToolStatus::MissingApiKey => (true, false, None),\n499\t                            detection::ToolStatus::IncompatibleVersion => {\n500\t                                // Extract missing feature from diagnostics\n501\t                                let feature = diagnostics\n502\t                                    .rejections\n503\t                                    .iter()\n504\t                                    .find(|r| r.tool_name == t.name || r.tool_name == t.name.replace(\"-code\", \"\"))\n505\t                                    .and_then(|r| match &r.reason {\n506\t                                        guidance::RejectionReason::IncompatibleVersion { missing_feature, .. } => {\n507\t                                            Some(missing_feature.clone())\n508\t                                        }\n509\t                                        _ => None,\n510\t                                    });\n511\t                                (false, true, feature)\n512\t                            }\n513\t                            _ => (false, false, None),\n514\t                        };\n515\t                        guidance::ToolFixInfo {\n516\t                            name: t.name.clone(),\n517\t                            version: t.version.clone(),\n518\t                            missing_api_key,\n519\t                            api_key_env_var: t.api_key_env_var.clone(),\n520\t                            incompatible_version,\n521\t                            missing_feature,\n522\t                        }\n523\t                    })\n524\t                    .collect();\n525\t\n526\t                if !not_ready.is_empty() {\n527\t                    eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_not_ready_guidance(&not_ready));\n528\t                }\n529\t                return Err(\"No ready tools available\".into());\n530\t            }\n531\t        }\n532\t    } else {\n533\t        // Interactive mode: show the TUI wizard for selection\n534\t        match wizard::run_wizard(tools.clone()) {\n535\t            Ok(Some(tool)) => {\n536\t                // User selected a tool\n537\t                eprintln!(\n538\t                    \"\\n✨ Using: {} ({})\",\n539\t                    tool.name,\n540\t                    tool.binary_path.display()\n541\t                );\n542\t                tool\n543\t            }\n544\t            Ok(None) => {\n545\t                // User chose \"Manual Setup\" - skip auto-configuration\n546\t                eprintln!(\"\\n📝 Manual setup selected.\");\n547\t                eprintln!(\"   Create ~/.forge/config.yaml manually to configure FORGE.\");\n548\t                return Ok(());\n549\t            }\n550\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::UserCancelled) => {\n551\t                eprintln!(\"\\n👋 Setup cancelled.\");\n552\t                return Err(\"User cancelled setup\".into());\n553\t            }\n554\t            Err(wizard::WizardError::NoToolsAvailable) => {\n555\t                // This shouldn't happen since we already checked, but handle it\n556\t                eprint!(\"{}\", guidance::generate_guidance(Some(&diagnostics)));\n557\t                return Err(\"No compatible CLI tools available\".into());\n558\t            }\n559\t            Err(e) => {\n560\t                eprintln!(\"\\nerror: Wizard failed: {}\", e);\n561\t                return Err(format!(\"Wizard failed: {}\", e).into());\n562\t            }\n563\t        }\n564\t    };\n565\t\n566\t    if non_interactive {\n567\t        // Only print in non-interactive mode (wizard already prints in interactive mode)\n568\t        info!(\n569\t            \"Auto-selected: {} ({})\",\n570\t            selected_tool.name,\n571\t            selected_tool.binary_path.display()\n572\t        );\n573\t    }\n574\t\n575\t    // Create directory structure\n576\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n577\t    if !non_interactive {\n578\t        eprintln!(\"\\n📁 Creating directory structure...\");\n579\t    }\n580\t    generator::create_directory_structure(&forge_dir)?;\n581\t\n582\t    // Generate config.yaml\n583\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n584\t    if !non_interactive {\n585\t        eprintln!(\"📝 Generating config.yaml...\");\n586\t    }\n587\t    generator::generate_config_yaml(&selected_tool, &config_path)?;\n588\t\n589\t    // Generate launcher script\n590\t    let launcher_name = format!(\"{}-launcher\", selected_tool.name);\n591\t    let launcher_path = forge_dir.join(\"launchers\").join(&launcher_name);\n592\t    if !non_interactive {\n593\t        eprintln!(\"🚀 Generating launcher script...\");\n594\t    }\n595\t    generator::generate_launcher_script(&selected_tool, &launcher_path)?;\n596\t\n597\t    if !non_interactive {\n598\t        eprintln!(\"\\n✅ Configuration complete!\");\n599\t        eprintln!(\"   Config: {}\", config_path.display());\n600\t        eprintln!(\"   Launcher: {}\", launcher_path.display());\n601\t    }\n602\t\n603\t    info!(\n604\t        \"Onboarding complete: using {} backend\",\n605\t        selected_tool.name\n606\t    );\n607\t    Ok(())\n608\t}\n609\t\n610\t/// Normalize backend name for comparison.\n611\t///\n612\t/// Maps common aliases to canonical names:\n613\t/// - \"claude\", \"claude-code\", \"claudecode\" -> \"claude-code\"\n614\t/// - \"opencode\" -> \"opencode\"\n615\t/// - \"aider\" -> \"aider\"\n616\tfn normalize_backend_name(name: &str) -> String {\n617\t    let lower = name.to_lowercase();\n618\t    match lower.as_str() {\n619\t        \"claude\" | \"claude-code\" | \"claudecode\" => \"claude-code\".to_string(),\n620\t        other => other.to_string(),\n621\t    }\n622\t}\n623\t\n624\t/// Handle the `forge init` command.\n625\tfn handle_init_command(non_interactive: bool, force: bool, reconfigure: bool, detect_tools: bool) -> ExitCode {\n626\t    info!(\n627\t        \"Handling init command (non_interactive={}, force={}, reconfigure={}, detect_tools={})\",\n628\t        non_interactive, force, reconfigure, detect_tools\n629\t    );\n630\t\n631\t    // Handle --detect-tools: dry run that only shows detection results\n632\t    if detect_tools {\n633\t        return handle_detect_tools_command();\n634\t    }\n635\t\n636\t    let forge_dir = get_forge_dir();\n637\t    let config_path = forge_dir.join(\"config.yaml\");\n638\t\n639\t    // Handle --reconfigure: backup existing config before re-running setup\n640\t    if reconfigure {\n641\t        if !config_path.exists() {\n642\t            if non_interactive {\n643\t                eprintln!(\"error: No configuration found to reconfigure\");\n644\t                eprintln!(\"Use 'forge init' to create initial configuration\");\n645\t            } else {\n646\t                eprintln!(\"No configuration found. Running first-time setup instead...\\n\");\n647\t            }\n648\t            // Fall through to normal setup since there's nothing to reconfigure\n649\t        } else {\n650\t            // Backup existing config before proceeding\n651\t            if let Err(e) = backup_config(&forge_dir, &config_path) {\n652\t                eprintln!(\"❌ Failed to backup config: {}\", e);\n653\t                return ExitCode::from(1);\n654\t            }\n655\t            if !non_interactive {\n656\t                eprintln!(\"📦 Existing configuration backed up\\n\");\n657\t            }\n658\t        }\n659\t    } else if !force && config_path.exists() {\n660\t        // Neither --force nor --reconfigure: don't overwrite existing config\n661\t        if non_interactive {\n662\t            eprintln!(\n663\t                \"error: Configuration already exists at {}\",\n664\t                config_path.display()\n665\t            );\n666\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite existing configuration\");\n667\t            eprintln!(\"Use --reconfigure to backup and re-run setup\");\n668\t            return ExitCode::from(1);\n669\t        } else {\n670\t            eprintln!(\n671\t                \"Configuration already exists at {}\",\n672\t                config_path.display()\n673\t            );\n674\t            eprintln!(\"Use --force to overwrite      }\n704\t    }\n705\t}\n706\t\n707\t/// Backup existing config.yaml before reconfiguration.\n708\t///\n709\t/// Creates a timestamped backup to preserve user's previous settings.\n710\t/// Keeps Default users:\");\n1181\t            eprintln!(\"     - admin/admin123 (Admin)\");\n1182\t            eprintln!(\"     - operator/operator123 (Operator)\");\n1183\t            eprintln!(\"     -
